There is no limit to how many tests your child can take.\r\n\r\nThe Year 3 Maths PRO App covers 6 topics that include 26 subtopics which cover the Year 3 syllabus in the UK.\r\n\r\nEach subtopic has 10 questions which make up a test.  \r\nAt the end of the test the child is rewarded with an award.\r\nA diamond for 100% \r\nA gold star for 90 to 100%\r\nA silver star for 70 to 90%\r\nA bronze star for 50 to 70%\r\nA red star for less than 50%\r\n\r\nUp to 10 awards per subtopic can be displayed.
